[\[39a.1\]]shar dang /_byang dang /_nub dang /_lho dang /_dbus kyis rnams dang /_thog rnams kyi kha dog dkar po dang /_ljang gu dang /_dmar po dang /_ser po dang /_nag po'o/_/gzhan ni re khA lnga dang /_sa gzhi dang /_thog rnams nag po dang /_ljang gu dang /_dmar po dang /_ser po dang /_
[\[39a.2\]]dkar po dang bsres pa'i sngon po'i mdog go zhes zer ro/_/de bzhin du snga ma dang /_phyi mar kha dog gi rim pa yongs su bsams nas rdul tshon dgye bar bya'o/_/de yang skal ba dang mi ldan pa 'dus na mtshan ma dang phyag rgya ji ltar rigs par bri'o/_/skal ba dang mi ldan pa med na ni lha'i sku bri bar
[\[39a.3\]]bya zhing /_bris sku'am/_lugs ma'am/_'bur du btod pa'am/_legs par 'dus byas pa gzhag par bya'o/_/de ltar klu'i blo'i zhabs kyis/_ji ltar nus pas dkyil 'khor du/_/sa bon dgod bya yang na ni/_/mtshan ma'am lha yi gzugs nyid de/_/lugs ma'am bzo byas dgod par
[\[39a.4\]]bya/_/zhes gsungs so/_/phyag rgya bri ba ni mngon par brjod pa'i rgyud bla ma las gsungs te/_mi nus na ni bris pa yi/_/phyag rgya'am mtshan ma dgod par bya'o/_/gang yang gsungs pa/_tshon nam yang na pir rnams kyis/_/bris pa rnams kyis rnam par spras/_/zhes so/_/dpal kha sbyor gyi
[\[39a.5\]]rgyud du yang /_de ltar lugs ma dang /_'dus byas pa la sogs pa'i gzugs dang /_mtshan ma'i phyag rgya dang ldan pa'o zhes gsungs so/_/de'i phyir 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor la/_lte bar bcom ldan 'das 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i zla ba ral gri sngo bsangs so/_/shar du zla ba la rnam par
[\[39a.6\]]snang mdzad kyi 'khor lo dkar po rtsibs brgyad pa'o/_/lhor nyi ma la rin chen 'byung ldan gyi rin po che ljang gu cha dgu pa'o/_/nub tu nyi ma la mgon po 'od dpag med kyi pad+ma dmar po 'dab ma brgyad pa'o/_/byang du nyi ma la don yod grub pa'i ral gyi ljang gu'o/_/mer zla ba la spyan ma'i mig 'bras
[\[39a.7\]]nag po can gyi mig dkar po gnyis sprin la gnas pa'o/_/bden bral du zla ba la mA ma kI'i rdo rje nag po rtse lnga pa ste rgyud du de ltar bshad pa'i phyir ro/_/rlung du zla ba la gos dkar mo'i pad+ma dmar po kha bye ba yu ba dang rtsa ba dang bcas pa'o/_/dbang ldan du zla ba la sgrol ma'i ut+pal mdog sngo ser ro/_/
[\[39b\]]
[\[39b.1\]]me la sogs pa'i mtshams bzhi dang /_shar sgo'i g.yon dang g.yas su cha chung gnyis gnyis spangs pa'i 'gram dag tu zla ba rnams la go rims bzhin du gzugs dang sgra dang /_dri dang /_ro dang /_reg bya dang /_chos kyi dbyings kyi rdo rje ma rnams kyi me long dkar po dang /_dri za'i pi wang sngon po dang
[\[39b.2\]]dri ser po'i dung dang /_ro'i snod dmar po dang /_ras sna tshogs dang /_chos 'byung dkar po'o/_/shar la sogs pa'i sgor nyi ma rnams la gshin rje mthar byed dang /_shes rab mthar byed dang /_pad+ma mthar byed dang bgegs mthar byed kyi go rims bzhin du rdo rje tho ba nag po dang /_rdo rjes mtshan
[\[39b.3\]]pa'i dbyug pa dkar po dang /_pad+ma dmar po dang /_rdo rje kha gyes pa sngon po'o/_/'dir zla ba dang nyi ma bcu dgu ni sna tshogs pad+ma la gnas pa'o/_/mtshan ma thams cad ni 'od zer dang bcas pa rang rang gi phyogs su mgo bstan pa'o/_/'khor lo'i dbang phyug ni mgo nub tu bstan pa'o/_/de ltar
[\[39b.4\]]phyi ma rnams su yang ngo /_/rdo rje sems dpa' 'khor lo'i dbang phyug nyid la ni dbus su chu skyes dang zla ba la ni zhi ba'i rdo rje sngon po'o/_/kha cig ni sna tshogs rdo rje'o zhes so/_/mkhas pa rnams ni dbus kyi 'od zer gyi thig zlum po la tshon gyis re khA mi bya'o zhes so/_/zlum po'i thig gi phyi ngos su
[\[39b.5\]]tshangs pa'i thig gi glo so sor cha chung bzhi dor nas bum pa cha chung bzhi pa ste/_bdud rtsis bkang pa'i gsar gyi bum pa cha brgyad do zhes phyogs gcig go/_/gzhan ni rin po che'i rang bzhin rang gi phyogs kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i mdog go zhes so/_/'di dang phyi ma rnams la dbus su de bzhin
[\[39b.6\]]gshegs pa gzhan pa'i mtshan ma dgod pa ni/_de'i dbus su dbus kyi mtshan ma bri bar bya'o/_/bsdus pa'i rim par gsungs pa'i dkyil 'khor la/_dbus su nyi ma la mi bskyod pa'i rdo rje kha gyes pa rtse lnga pa in+d+ra nI la lta bu dang /_reg bya rdo rje ma'i sna tshogs pa'i gos so/_/rnam par
[\[39b.7\]]snang mdzad la sogs pa'i rim pa dang po dang gnyis par gnas pa bcu gnyis po rnams kyi mtshan ma rnams ni snga ma bzhin no/_/rim pa gsum pa'i sgo'i 'gram gyi snam bu la tshangs pa'i thig nas cha chung bzhi dor bar g.yon du byams pa'i klu shing gi me tog gi 'khor lo dang bcas pa'o/_/

[\[40a.1\]]g.yas su sa'i snying po'i 'khor lo rtsibs brgyad pa dkar po'o/_/lhor de bzhin du phyag na rdo rje'i dang /_nam mkha'i snying po'i rdo rje dang /_rin po che margata cha dgu pa'o/_/nub tu de bzhin du 'jig rten dbang phyug dang /_'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi pad+ma dmar po dang rdo rje'o/_/byang du

[\[40b.1\]]sha k+ti'o/_/rlung dus rdo rje ma'i bum pa dkar ljang ngo /_/rim pa gsum par shar gyi phyogs su bzhad ma'i rdo rje kha dog dmar po'o/_/lhor sgeg ma'i 'khar rnga'o/_/nub tu glu ma'i 'khor rnga'o/_/byang du gar ma'i rdo rje rtse gsum pa ljang gu'o/_/dbang ldan du gling bu ma'i gling bu'o/_/mer pi wang

[\[67a.3\]]na yang ltung ba med do zhes 'dul bar bstan pa de rtogs par bya'o/_/gal te phyogs kyi bye brag skye bo ngan pa'i spyod yul du gyur na/_de'i tshe de la yang ye shes kyi phyag rgyas gsang ba dang shes rab ye shes kyi dbang sbyin par bya'o/_/skye bo ngan pa med na ni las kyi phyag rgya kho nas so/_/
[\[67a.4\]]de kho na nyid la mos pa mi brtan pa'i dge slong la ni dad pa dang ldan yang phyi'i shes rab ma'i dbang bzung ba bkag ste/_gzhan du sdom pa lnga ma nyams pas de don med pa chen por 'gyur ro/_/gal te yang bla ma bsgom pa la brtan par gyur na de'i tshe de la yang des gtad pa'i ye shes

[\[82b.1\]]sgor ni thal sbyor ba/_/gdugs bcas dbab cing 'di brjod bya/_/rgyud rnams 'dzin par 'gyur ba yi/_/slob ma 'di ni phul ba lags/_/zhes pas dkyil 'khor gyi dbang phyug la gsol ba gdab la/_gdugs gzhan du bzhag slob ma'i snying la 'bab pa brjod par bya ste/_da ni khyod nyid

[\[83a.1\]]ga'o/_/de ltar dbang thob cing dbugs phyung ste/_dga' ba'i slob mas de ltar bgyi'o/_/deng bdag skye ba 'bras bur bcas/_/bdag gi gson pa'ang 'bras bur bcas/_/de ring sangs rgyas rigs su skyes/_/sangs rgyas sras su deng bdag 'gyur/_/zhes brjod

[\[83b\]]
[\[83b.1\]]'byung ba'i bdag po chos 'byung rtogs par bya ba'i ched du chos 'byung gsal bar byed pa'i dril bu sgra dang bcas pas dbang bskur ba'o/_/bdag po'i ched du dbang ni bdag po'i dbang du yang brjod do/_/ma 'ongs pa na thub pa'i go 'phang gi ming du 'os pa'i sa bon dgod pa'i don du ming gi dbang
[\[83b.2\]]ngo /_/chu'i dbang la sogs pa lnga po 'di rnams rim pa bzhin chos kyi dbyings rnam par dag pa dang mnyam pa nyid dang so sor rtog pa dang bya ba grub pa dang /_me long lta bu'i ye shes kyi sa bon yongs su rgyas par byed pa'i phyir de'i bdag nyid du mos par bya'o/_/chu'i dbang ni me long lta bu'i ye shes kyi bdag
[\[83b.3\]]nyid du yang de nyid bsdus pa las gsungs te/_mi bskyod pa yang me long lta bu'i ye shes kyi bdag nyid du yang ngo /_/'di nas brtsams te rnam par dag pa zung 'jug gi byang chub rtogs par bya ba'i ched du brtson par gyis shig ces nges par bya bar dgongs nas de'i rang bzhin gyi rdo rje 'dzin pa'i nges pa ni rdo rje'i
[\[83b.4\]]dam tshig go/_/chos kyi phung po brgyad khri bzhi stong rab tu ston pa'i rgyu de bzhin nyid rtogs pa la sbyar ba'i ched du sgra dang bcas pa'i dril bu'i dam tshig go/_/shes rab dang thabs kyi rang bzhin bde ba chen po'i bdag nyid rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rang bzhin shin tu brtan par rung ba nyid du bsgrub pa'i phyir
[\[83b.5\]]phyag rgya'i dam tshig go/_/de nyid kyi phyir mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur las dam tshig gnyis kyi 'khor can phyag rgya'i dam tshig kho nas rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi dbang du gsungs so/_/rgyud gzhan du ni dam tshig gsum slob dpon gyi dbang gi 'khor du gsungs so/_/de ltar yang sngar shes rab bcu drug
[\[83b.6\]]ces pa la sogs pa gsungs so/_/dri ma 'khrud par rung ba nyid ni dam tshig rnam par gzhag pa gnyis ka la yod par mi 'gal lo/_/ji ltar sa bcu pa la phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa' chen po rnams phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis dbang bskur ba de bzhin du dam tshig

[\[84a\]]

[\[88a.1\]]kyis brgyan par blugs te glang po che'i steng ngam/_khyogs la bzhag la yon bdag gis byin pa'i ras kyis brgyan pa'i rnal 'byor mas bzung ba'i 'do li la zhon pa'i slob dpon nam slob mas dril bu'i sgra dang /_bkra shis kyi glu dang /_rol mo'i sgra dang /_gdugs dang /_rgyal mtshan

[\[94a.1\]]sgrog ma dang /_gzhan gyis mi thub ma rnams so/_/phyogs gzhan gyi ra rnams la ni dbus su ye shes mkha' 'gro ma dang /_shar du rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma dang /_byang du mkha' 'gro ma drag mo dang /_nub tu rdo rje ro langs ma dang /_lhor gtum mo'o/_/dril bu'i steng du kha 'og tu

[\[94a.7\]]pa'i dkur bzung ba'am gsor zhing /_oM badzra d+harmA ra Ni ta pra ra Ni ta saM pra ra ni ta sarba bud+d+ha k+She tra pra tsA li ni pra dz+nyA pa ra mi tA nA da saM b+ha be badzra satwa hr-i da yaM san+to Sha ni hUM hUM hUM ho ho ho swA hA/_zhes brjod cing dril bu dbus kyi phyogs brgyad rnams su lce bskyod pas dkrol bar bya'o/_/dril bu dang rdo rje'i dbye ba

[\[94b.1\]]rnams kyi mtshan nyid la sogs pa rgyas par ni man ngag gi snye mar brjod do zhes pa/_rdo rje dang dril bu'i mtshan nyid la sogs pa'i cho ga'o/_/de ltar thub pa mchog rnams kyi ni gsung gi rgya mtsho zab mo ru/_/kha cig thos pa tsam yang mi 'jug 'ga' zhig gis kyang gting ma rnyed/_/snying rje dang bcas blo

[\[95a.1\]]bcom ldan 'das kyis spro ba dang bsdu ba'i byed pa po/_/rnam pa kun gyi mchog ldan pa/_/ye shes skad cig gis rdzogs pa/_/rdzogs pa'i rnal 'byor zhes brjod do/_/zhes gsungs so/_/de yang bdag dang sems can thams cad rdo rje 'dzin pa nyid thob par 'dod
[\[95a.2\]]pa'i spro ba dang ldan pas/_phung po dang khams dang skye mched la sogs pa gzugs brnyan lta bur stong pa nyid dang ro gcig par nges par byas nas/_'od rab tu gsal ba la rab tu zhugs te/_skad cig gi yan lag dang bcas pa'i gzhal yas khang gi dbus su dkyil 'khor dang dkyil 'khor pas yongs
[\[95a.3\]]su bskor ba'i dpal rdo rje sems dpa' dang 'jam pa'i rdo rje la sogs pa'i sku stong pa nyid dang /_snying rje ro gcig pa'i bde ba chen po'i rang bzhin rigs kyi bdag pos dbu brgyan cing thugs ka'i sa bon dang ldan pa la de bzhin gshegs pa dang /_lha mo dang /_byang chub sems dpa' dang /_khro bo la
[\[95a.4\]]sogs pa dpag tu med pa spros te/_ji ltar gzhan la phan par nus pa'i chos ston pa la sogs pas gzhan bsod nams kyi tshogs mthar phyin pa la gzhag cing /_bsdu ba byas pas bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i skur bskyed par bya'o/_/de la 'di'i yan lag la sogs pa ni sa 'og gi mthar thug par
[\[95a.5\]]ji ltar mngon par 'dod pa'i rgyar/_gcig tu sra zhing mkhregs la 'bar ba'i rdo rje'i rang bzhin gyis sa gzhi dang bskal pa'i mtha'i me 'bar ba'i 'od zer gyi phreng ba dang ldan pas mtshams bcing ba dang /_sa 'og nas steng gi bar du shin tu mtho zhing mkhregs la sra zhing 'bar ba'i rdo rje ra ba dang /_rdo rje'i ra

[\[95a.7\]]la gshin rje mthar byed nag po/_zhal dkar po dang dmar po rdo rje'i tho ba nag po dang ral gri dang nor bu dang pad+ma 'dzin pa'o/_/lho'i rtsibs la shes rab mthar byed dkar po zhal nag po dang dmar po/_rdo rjes mtshan pa'i dbyug pa dkar po dang /_ral gri dang /_nor bu dang pad+ma 'dzin pa'o/_/nub
[\[95b\]]
[\[95b.1\]]kyi rtsibs la pad+ma mthar byed dmar po zhal sngon po dang dkar po/_pad+ma dmar po dang ral gri dang nor bu dang 'khor lo 'dzin pa'o/_/byang gi rtsibs la bgegs mthar byed nag po zhal dkar po dang dmar po khro bo'i rdo rje dang ral gri dang nor bu dang pad+ma 'dzin pa'o/_/mer 'dod pa'i rgyal po sngon po zhal
[\[95b.2\]]dkar po dang dmar po/_lcags kyu dang ral gri dang nor bu dang mtsho skyes 'dzin pa'o/_/bden bral du dbyug pa sngon po nag po zhal dkar po dang dmar po dbyug pa sngon po dang ral gri dang nor bu dang chu skyes 'dzin pa'o/_/rlung du stobs po che nag po zhal dkar po dang dmar po/_rtse gsum pa dang ral
[\[95b.3\]]gri dang nor bu dang pad+ma bsnams pa'o/_/dbang ldan du mi g.yo ba sngon po zhal dkar po dang dmar po ral gri dang nor bu dang pad+ma 'dzin pa'o/_/steng du gtsug tor 'khor los sgyur ba ser po zhal sngon po dang dmar po/_'khor lo ser po dang ral gri dang nor bu dang pad+ma 'dzin pa'o/_/'og tu gnod
[\[95b.4\]]mdzes rgyal po sngon po zhal dkar po dang dmar po rdo rje dang ral gri dang nor bu dang pad+ma bsnams pa'o/_/de la gtsug tor dang 'dod pa'i rgyal po dang mi g.yo ba dang gnod mdzes rnams ni rin po che'i cod pan can/_rin po che sna tshogs kyis brgyan par gyur pa/_mche ba cung zad gtsigs pa ston
[\[95b.5\]]pa/_sma ra dang bral ba'o/_/de las gzhan pa rnams ni mi sdug pa'i gzugs can smin ma 'khyog pa dang bcas pas dbu skra dmar ser gyen du brdzes pa/_smin ma dang sma ra dmar ser dang bcas pa/_zhal gdangs pa/_mche ba gtsigs pa/_ljags 'gyur ba/_gad rgyangs dang

[\[95b.7\]]khros pa dang 'bar bas shin tu 'jigs pa bskal pa 'jig pa'i dus kyi me lta bu'i 'od dang ldan pa'i rang gi sku'i sprul pa dpag tu med pa'i tshogs kyis kyang khams gsum mtha' yas pa na gnas pa'i bgegs kyi tshogs ma lus pa yang dang yang du brlag par byed pa phyag drug pa rtsa ba'i
[\[96a\]]
[\[96a.1\]]phyag dag gis rang dang 'dra ba'i shes rab ma la 'khyud pa/_zhal gsum pa khyad par du rtsa ba'i zhal gyi mdog ni sku mdog lta bu ste/_g.yas pa dang g.yon pa yi ni gong du brjod do/_/zhal re re la'ang dmar la zlum pa'i spyan gsum mo/_/'khor lo yang rgyun mi 'chad par
[\[96a.2\]]drag tu 'khor bas brtan par gnas pa lta bur 'bar ba'i tshogs dpag tu med pa 'phro ba'o/_/de'i lte ba'i nang du 'og gi rtsibs kyi steng du chos 'byung gru gsum dkar po shin tu yangs pa'i nang du 'og gi zur la gnas pa'i sna tshogs pad+ma'i steng du sna tshogs rdo rje dang bcas pa'o/_/rdo rje de'i phyogs
[\[96a.3\]]kyi ra rnams dang lte ba ni ji ltar rigs par rnam par snang mdzad la sogs pa'i mdog dang 'dra ba'o/_/der rin po che kha dog lnga las yongs su rdzogs pa thub pa'i dbang po'i dkyil 'khor 'od gsal ba phyogs kyi 'khor lo thams cad sna tshogs pa'i 'od zer gyis khyab pa'i gzhal yas khang ngo /_/de'i
[\[96a.4\]]dbus su bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje sems dpa' 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i sku gur gum gyi mdog lta bu g.yas dang g.yon gyi zhal nag po dang dkar po/_rtsa ba'i phyag dag gis rang dang 'dra ba'i shes rab ma la 'khyud pa/_ral gri dang mda' dang ut+pal dang gzhu 'dzin pa rin po che'i cod pan can no/_/rin po
[\[96a.5\]]che sna tshogs pas brgyan pa/_'od zer mtha' yas pa'o/_/de'i shar gyi phyogs su rnam par snang mdzad dkar po g.yas ba dang cig shos kyi zhal nag po dang dmar po phyag rnams na 'khor lo rtsibs brgyad pa dkar po dang /_ral gri dang nor bu dang pad+ma'o/_/lhor rin chen 'byung ldan ser po rin po che
[\[96a.6\]]margata zur dgu pa dang /_ral gri dang 'khor lo dang pad+ma 'dzin pa'o/_/nub tu snang ba mtha' yas dmar po pad+ma dmar po dang ral gri dang nor bu dang /_'khor lo 'dzin pa'o/_/byang du don yod grub pa ljang gu ral gri dang 'khor lo dang nor bu dang pad+ma 'dzin pa'o/_/'di gsum gyi g.yas pa dang
[\[96a.7\]]cig shos kyi zhal ni nag po dang dkar po'o/_/de bzhin gshegs pa 'di dag thams cad rin po che'i cod pan dang ldan pa rin po che sna tshogs kyis brgyan pa'o/_/mer spyan ma rnam snang dang mtshungs pa'o/_/bden bral du mA ma kI mi bskyod pa lta bu ut+pal dmar po dang /_ral gri dang nor bu dang pad+ma
[\[96b\]]
[\[96b.1\]]'dzin pa ste/_sgrub thabs thams cad las de ltar bshad pa'i phyir ro/_/rlung du gos dkar mo snang ba mtha' yas dang mtshungs pa'o/_/dbang ldan du sgrol ma rin chen 'byung ldan lta bu ut+pal ser po dang ral gri dang nor bu dang pad+ma 'dzin pa'o/_/dbus kyi rim pa las phyi rol du me'i mtshams
[\[96b.2\]]su gzugs rdo rje ma rnam par snang mdzad lta bu rin po che'i me long dang ral gri dang nor bu dang chu skyes 'dzin pa'o/_/srin por sgra rdo rje ma mi bskyod pa lta bu pi wang sngon po dang ral gri dang nor bu dang pad+ma 'dzin pa'o/_/rlung du dri rdo rje ma rin chen 'byung ldan lta bu dri chab kyi dung ser po dang ral gri dang 'khor lo dang
[\[96b.3\]]chu skyes 'dzin pa'o/_/dbang ldan du ro rdo rje ma snang ba mtha' yas dang mtshungs pa ro'i snod dmar po dang ral gri dang nor bu dang 'khor lo 'dzin pa'o/_/shar sgo'i g.yon logs su reg bya rdo rje ma don yod grub pa dang mtshungs pa gos sna tshogs dang ral gri dang nor bu dang chu skyes 'dzin pa'o/_/
[\[96b.4\]]shar sgo'i g.yas logs su chos kyi dbyings kyi rdo rje ma rdo rje sems dpa' dang mtshungs pa chos 'byung dkar po dang ral gri dang nor bu dang chu skyes 'dzin pa'o/_/'jam pa'i rdo rje la sogs pa'i lha 'di rnams ni zhal gsum pa phyag drug pa phyag mtshan dang po gnyis ni g.yas pa dag gis so/_/
[\[96b.5\]]gzhan gnyis ni g.yon pa dag gis 'dzin pa'o/_/thams cad kyi rtsa ba'i zhal ni sku mdog bzhin no/_/shar la sogs pa'i sgo ru gshin rje mthar byed dang shes rab mthar byed dang pad+ma mthar byed dang bgegs mthar byed rnams so/_/'jam pa'i rdo rje dang rnam par snang mdzad dang lha mo bcu po
[\[96b.6\]]rnams ni zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la rdo rje skyil krung gis bzhugs pa'o/_/gzhan ni nyi ma la'o/_/zla ba dang nyi ma'i 'og tu sna tshogs pad+ma'o/_/de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi gtso bo'i phyag dag gis rang 'od kyi shes rab dag la 'khyud pa ste de bzhin du shes rab rnams 'od kyi thabs la'o/_/dbu
[\[96b.7\]]la rigs kyi bdag po ste 'jam pa'i rdo rje la sogs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams dang /_mA ma kI dang sgra rdo rje ma dang /_srung ba'i 'khor lo'i khro bo brgyad la ni mi bskyod pa'o/_/spyan ma dang gzugs rdo rje ma dang gshin rje gshed rnams la ni rnam par snang mdzad do/_/dri rdo rje ma la ni rin
[\[97a\]]
[\[97a.1\]]chen 'byung ldan no/_/gos dkar mo dang ro rdo rje ma dang pad+ma mthar byed rnams la 'od dpag med do/_/sgrol ma dang reg bya rdo rje ma la ni don yod grub pa'o/_/chos kyi dbyings kyi rdo rje ma la ni rdo rje 'dzin pa'o/_/gzhan ni mi bskyod pa'o/_/'dir rdo rje sems dpa' ni sku mdog dkar
[\[97a.2\]]po la cung zad dmar po'i mdangs dang ldan pa g.yas pa dang cig shos kyi zhal ni sngon po dang dmar po gtso bo'i phyag dag gis rang 'od kyi shes rab la 'khyud pa rdo rje sngon po dang ral gri dang nor bu dang pad+ma 'dzin pa/_sna tshogs pad+ma dang /_zla ba'i gdan la rdo rje skyil krung gis bzhugs pa zla ba'i mdog can rin
[\[97a.3\]]po che'i cod pan dang /_rin po che'i rgyan dang ldan pa dbul mi bskyod pas rgyas btab pa'o/_/'dir 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i thugs kar dam tshig sems dpa' lta bu'i ye shes sems dpa' de'i thugs kar zla bar ral gri'i yu ba la gnas pa'i sa bon maM ngo /_/rtag pa dang rin 'byung dang /_'od dpag
[\[97a.4\]]med dang don yod grub pa dang mi bskyod pa rnams kyi thugs kar phyag mtshan la ji ltar rigs par zla ba'am/_nyi ma la/_b+h+rUM/_AM/_dzrAM/_khaM/_hUM ngo /_spyan la sogs pa'i lha mo rnams la lAM mAM pAM tAM/_dzaHhUM baM hoHkhaM raM maM/_khro bo rnams la hUM ngo /_/lha thams cad kyi snying po'i sngags ni rdo rje'i phreng bar bshad
[\[97a.5\]]do/_/'dir rdzogs pa'i rnal 'byor du mig la sogs pa byin gyis brlab pa dang ye shes sems dpa' dgug gzhug la sogs pa ni ma bshad do/_/de med kyang mig gi mngon par shes pa la sogs pa'i yon tan gyi tshogs dpag tu med cing bsam gyis mi khyab pas mdzes par byas pa'i yi dam gyi lha'i
[\[97a.6\]]sku cig car kho na la legs par yongs su dag cing rnam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs par rgyun du yang dang yang lhag par mos pa brtan par bya'o/_/snying po'i sngags la sogs pa bstan pa ni bum pa lhag par gnas pa la sogs pa la nye bar mkho ba'i ched du'o/_/gang gi tshe dbus su de bzhin gshegs
[\[97a.7\]]pa gzhan gtso bor gyur pa de'i dbus su gnas pa gzhan de'i gnas su dgod do/_/'od dpag med dkar por yang 'gyur te/_chos rnams dkar po'i rang bzhin gyis/_/'dir ni ngag gi dbang phyug dkar/_/zhes gsungs pa'i phyir/_'di dang 'chad pa'i dkyil 'khor rnams su gang gi dkyil
[\[97b\]]
[\[97b.1\]]'khor ba'i lha'i gtso bo'i gnas gang du bshad pa de nyid du gtso bo de dkyil 'khor gyi dbang po la mngon par phyogs shing de dang 'khyud pa ni de la mngon du phyogs pa nyid de gzhan gyi gnas su phyin pa'i phyir ro/_/'dir ni gzhal yas khang gi yan lag rnam pa gsum ste/_rdo rje'i sa gzhi la sogs
[\[97b.2\]]pas yongs su bskor ba'i rdo rje'i gur dang /_srung ba'i 'khor lo dang /_chos 'byung ngo /_/de la rdo rje'i gur ni 'chad par 'gyur ba'i gzhal yas khang thams cad la'o/_/srung ba'i 'khor lo dang /_chos 'byung ni 'ga' zhig kho na la 'chad do/_/bri bar bya ba'i gzhal yas khang rnams la ni chos kyi
[\[97b.3\]]dbyings kyi ngo bo chos 'byung ngam chos kyi dbyings kyi khongs su chud par mtshon pa'i ched du rdo rje phreng ba bri bar bya'o/_/ji ltar phyi rol de bzhin nang /_zhes pas rdzogs rim gyi dkyil 'khor rtogs par bya ba'i ched du 'jig rten khams kyi 'khor yug mtshon pa'i phyir rdo rje phreng ba bri ba ni nges par ro/_/'dir srung
[\[97b.4\]]ba'i 'khor lo ni de ltar ma yin pas bri mi dgos te/_bgegs bzlog pa ni gzhan gyis kyang byed pas so/_/gzhan yang stong pa nyid kho na/_bcom ldan 'das kyis bgegs kyi tshogs ma lus pa rtsa ba dang bcas pa brlag par byed pa'i nus pa rab tu gyur pas/_de la lhag par mos pa brtan pa nyid
[\[97b.5\]]bskyed pa'i ched du bri ba'i dkyil 'khor la srung ba'i 'khor lo bri bar ma bstan to/_/bsgom bya'i dkyil 'khor la yang kha cig tu bsgom par gsungs pa las thams cad du ma yin no/_/bgegs bsal ba'i rjes la stong pa nyid la rab tu zhugs pas bsgom par bya ba'i dkyil 'khor la srung ba'i
[\[97b.6\]]'khor lo med de de'i phyir mi 'dri'o zhe na de ltar na khor yug mtshon pa'i rdo rje'i ra ba yang mi 'dri bar 'gyur ro/_/yang na gzhal yas khang bskyed pa'i dus su de yang bskyed do zhe na/_ma yin te/_bcom ldan 'das kyis rdo rje ra ba lan gsum bskyed par ni gang nas kyang ma gsungs so/_/lan gnyis
[\[97b.7\]]bskyed pas ci zhig bya cig car rdzogs pa nyid kyang rdo rje'i sa gzhi dang mtshams bcing ba dang rdo rje'i ra ba la sogs kun brtags mtha' dag stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin sgyu ma'i ngo bor gnas pa nyid do/_/des ni srung ba'i 'khor lo yod kyang dkyil 'khor du mi 'dri ba'i 'thad pa brjod pa nyid do/_/kha
[\[98a\]]
[\[98a.1\]]cig ni kha cig la srung ba'i 'khor lo bri bar bya'o zhes 'dod do zhes bya ba ni 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor ro//_//bsdus pa'i rim par gsungs pa'i dkyil 'khor la ni gzhal yas khang gi bar du snga ma bzhin no/_/khro bo rnams kyi khyad par ni bshad par bya'o/_/
[\[98a.2\]]gzhal yas khang gi dbus su mi bskyod pa nag po drag po g.yas pa dang cig shos kyi zhal dkar po dang dmar po phyag g.yas pa rnams ni khro bo'i rdo rje dang 'khor lo dang pad+ma bsnams pa/_g.yon pa rnams ni dril bu dang yid bzhin gyi nor bu dang ral gri 'dzin pa rang dang 'dra ba'i reg bya rdo rje ma la
[\[98a.3\]]'khyud pa'o/_/de'i shar la sogs pa'i phyogs rnams su rnam par snang mdzad la sogs pa dang /_me la sogs pa'i mtshams rnams su spyan ma la sogs pa'o/_/de la rnam par snang mdzad ni zhi ba dkar po'o/_/zhal dkar po dang nag po dang dmar po 'khor lo dang rdo rje dang pad+ma dkar po dang dril bu
[\[98a.4\]]dang nor bu dang ral gri 'dzin pa'o/_/bshad zin pa dang 'chad par 'gyur ba'i phyag mtshan dang po nas rim pa bzhin du phyag g.yas par steng nas 'og tu dang /_g.yon par 'og nas steng du rig par bya'o/_/rin chen 'byung ldan ni ser po ste zhal ser po dang nag po dang dkar po'o/_/zhal gyi mdog
[\[98a.5\]]gsum ni rim pa bzhin du rtsa ba dang g.yas pa dang g.yon yin no/_/nor bu dang rdo rje dang 'khor lo dang /_dril bu dang pad+ma ser po dang ral gri 'dzin pa'o/_/snang ba mtha' yas dmar po zhal dmar po dang nag po dang dkar po phyag g.yon pas dril bu dang bcas pa'i pad+ma dmar po'i yu ba thugs kar bzung
[\[98a.6\]]ba/_phyag g.yas pas kha 'byed pa'o/_/gzhan rnams kyis rdo rje dang 'khor lo dang rin po che dang /_ral gri 'dzin pa'o/_/don yod grub pa ni ljang gu zhal ljang gu dang nag po dang dkar po ral gri dang sna tshogs rdo rje dang 'khor lo dang dril bu dang pad+ma ljang gu dang nor bu 'dzin pa'o/_/de bzhin gshegs pa lnga
[\[98a.7\]]po 'di dang 'chad par 'gyur ba'i kun du bzang po'i bar ni ral pa'i thor cog dang rin po che'i cod pan dang rin po che la sogs pa'i rgyan sna tshogs kyis brgyan pa'o/_/spyan ma ni rnam par snang mdzad dang mtshungs pa ste/_'on kyang pad+ma dkar po'i gnas su ut+pal dkar po'o/_/mA ma kI ni mi bskyod pa lta bu
[\[98b\]]
[\[98b.1\]]ste 'on kyang pad+ma'i gnas su ut+pal sngon dmar ro/_/gos dkar mo ni snang ba mtha' yas dang mtshungs pa'o/_/sgrol ma ni don yod grub pa lta bu sna tshogs rdo rje dang 'khor lo dang ut+pal sdo ser dang dril bu dang nor bu rin po che dang ral gri 'dzin pa'o/_/rim pa gnyis par me'i mtshams su gzugs
[\[98b.2\]]rdo rje ma spyan ma lta bu ste 'on kyang dang po'i phyag dag gis me long dmar po 'dzin pa'o/_/bden bral du sgra rdo rje ma ser mo zhal ser po dang nag po dang dkar po dang ldan pa rtsa ba'i phyag gnyis kyis pi wang sngon mo bsgring ba'o/_/phyag lhag ma dag gis rdo rje dang ut+pal sngon mo dang rin po che dang ral gri 'dzin
[\[98b.3\]]pa'o/_/rlung du dri rdo rje ma ni gos dkar mo lta bu rtsa ba'i phyag gnyis kyis dri'i dung chos ser po 'dzin pa'o/_/dbang ldan du ro rdo rje ma ljang gu zhal ljang gu dang nag po dang dkar po phyag dang po gnyis ro'i snod dmar po 'dzin pa'o/_/lhag ma rnams kyis rdo rje dang 'khor lo dang rin po che dang ral gri 'dzin
[\[98b.4\]]pa'o/_/rim pa gsum pa'i shar gyi snam bu la byams pa dang sa'i snying po'o/_/lho'i snam bu la phyag na rdo rje dang nam mkha'i snying po'o/_/nub kyi snam bu la spyan ras gzigs dang 'jam pa'i dbyangs so/_/byang du sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel ba dang kun du bzang po'o/_/brgyad po 'di dag ni rang
[\[98b.5\]]gi rigs kyi bdag po dang mtshungs pa ste/_'on kyang byams pa ni rtsa ba'i phyag gis 'khor los mtshan pa'i yal ga dang bcas pa'i klu shing gi me tog 'dzin pa'o/_/shar la sogs pa'i sgo dang me la sogs pa'i mtshams dang steng dang 'og tu go rims bzhin du khro bo bcu'o/_/de la gshin rje gshed
[\[98b.6\]]ni nag po nag po dang dkar po dang dmar po rdo rje'i thob dang 'khor lo dang rdo rje dang thugs kar zhags pa dang bcas pa'i sdigs mdzub dang dril bu dang dgra s+t+wa 'dzin pa'o/_/shes rab mthar byed ni dkar po zhal dkar po dang nag po dang dmar po/_rdo rje dang rdo rjes mtshan pa'i dbyug pa dkar po dang /_ral
[\[98b.7\]]gri dang thugs kar zhags pa dang bcas pa'i sdigs mdzub dang dril bu dang dgra sta 'dzin pa'o/_/pad+ma mthar byed ni dmar po zhal dmar po dang nag po dang dkar po/_pad+ma dmar po dang ral gri dang gtun shing dang dril bu dang /_dgra sta dang zhags pa 'dzin pa'o/_/bgegs mthar byed
[\[99a\]]
[\[99a.1\]]ni sngon po zhal sngon po dang dkar po dang dmar po/_sna tshogs rdo rje dang 'khor lo dang gtun shing dang zhags pa dang bcas pa'i sdigs mdzub dang dril bu dang dgra sta 'dzin pa'o/_/mi g.yo ba ni sngon po zhal sngon po dang dkar po dang dmar po/_ral gri dang rdo rje dang
[\[99a.2\]]'khor lo dang sdigs mdzub dang dgra sta dang zhags pa 'dzin pa'o/_/'dod pa'i rgyal po ni sngon po zhal sngon po dang dkar po dang dmar po/_phyag gnyis kyis rdo rje hUM mdzad kyi phyag rgya 'dzin pa gzhan rnams kyis rdo rje dang ral gri dang zhags pa dang lcags kyu 'dzin pa'o/_/dbyug pa sngon po ni
[\[99a.3\]]nag po zhal nag po dang dkar po dang dmar po/_rdo rjes mtshan pa'i dbyug pa sngon po dang /_ral gri dang 'khor lo dang thugs kar zhags pa dang bcas pa'i sdigs mdzub dang pad+ma dang dgra sta 'dzin pa'o/_/stobs po che ni nag po zhal nag po dang dkar po dang dmar po rdo rjes mtshan pa'i dbyug pa
[\[99a.4\]]nag po dang ral gri dang 'khor lo dang thugs kar zhags pa dang bcas pa'i sdigs mdzub dang pad+ma dang dgra sta 'dzin pa'o/_/gtsug tor 'khor los sgyur ba ni nag po zhal nag po dang dkar po dang dmar po/_rtsa ba'i phyag dag gis gtsug tor spyi bor 'dzin pa'o/_/phyag lhag ma rnams kyis rdo rje dang
[\[99a.5\]]pad+ma dang sdigs mdzub dang ral gri rnams 'dzin pa'o/_/lag pa gnyis thal mo gan rkyal du mnyam par brkyang ba'i srin lag gnyis ni sen mo'i steng du mthe bo gnyis kyi sen mos mnan te mthe'u chung gnyis brkyang ngo /_/de bzhin du gung mo gnyis kyi sen mo mnyam par yang dag par rtse sprad la/_
[\[99a.6\]]mdzub mo gnyis dbus su rwa'i rnam pa ni kun du snang ba zhes bya ba gtsug tor gyi phyag rgya'o zhes kha cig go/_/'ga' zhig tu ni gzhan no/_/gnod mdzes rgyal po nag po zhal nag po dang dkar po dang dmar po/_rdo rje dang 'khor lo dang rin po che dang thugs kar zhags pa dang bcas pa'i sdigs mdzub
[\[99a.7\]]dang pad+ma dang ral gri 'dzin pa'o/_/mi bskyod pa la sogs pa 'di dag ni sna tshogs pad+ma'i steng du go rims bzhin du rdo rje rtse lnga pa dang 'khor lo dang rin po che ma ra ka ta cha dgu pa dang pad+ma dmar po dang sna tshogs rdo rje dang 'khor lo dang rdo rje dang pad+ma dang sna tshogs rdo rje dang klu shing gi me tog dang 'khor lo dang
[\[99b\]]
[\[99b.1\]]rdo rje dang rin po che dang /_pad+ma dang rdo rje dang sna tshogs rdo rje dang rdo rje dang thob dang rdo rje dang pad+ma dmar po dang sna tshogs rdo rje dang ral gri'i yu ba dang rdo rje dang rdo rjes mtshan pa'i dbyug pa sngon po dang dbyug pa nag po dang rdo rje dang rdo rje la gnas pa'i nyi ma dang zla ba la bzhugs pa zhal gsum phyag drug
[\[99b.2\]]pa'o/_/yang gzhan nas ni rang rang gi lha'i mdog lta bu'i rin po che las byas pa'o/_/de la rnam par snang mdzad dang lha mo rnams dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams zla ba la gnas pa'o/_/gzhan rnams ni nyi ma la gnas pa'o/_/mi bskyod pa la sogs pa rnams ni rdo rje'i skyil krung can no/_/
[\[99b.3\]]khro bo rnams ni zhabs g.yon brkyang pa g.yas bskum pa zhal so so la dmar la zlum pa'i spyan gsum gsum mnga' ba sgra sgrogs shing 'bar ba ste/_shin tu 'jigs pa srung ba'i 'khor lor brjod pa'i 'jigs pa'i gzugs la sogs pa'i khyad par dang ldan pa'o/_/'dir dkyil 'khor gyi
[\[99b.4\]]bdag po kho na yum dang bcas pa ste gnod mdzes kyi bar du lha gzhan rnams yum med pa'o/_/srung ba'i 'khor lo la gnas pa'i gshin rje gshed la sogs pa ni rang gi 'od kyi shes rab dang bcas pa ste de rnams ni go rims bzhin du rdo rje ro langs ma dang /_gzhan gyis mi thub ma dang khro gnyer can
[\[99b.5\]]dang ral pa gcig ma dang /_sna tshogs rdo rje ma dang /_sna tshogs rin chen ma dang /_sna tshogs pad+ma dang /_sna tshogs las ma dang /_nam mkha' rdo rje ma dang /_sa 'dzin ma rnams so/_/mi bskyod pa'i thugs kar ye shes sems dpa' phyag gnyis pa dmar po yum dang bcas pa'o/_/de'i thugs
[\[99b.6\]]kar ting nge 'dzin sems dpa' hUM nag po'o/_/rnam par snang mdzad kyi oM/_rin chen 'byung ldan gyi swA/_snang ba mtha' yas kyi AHdon yod grub pa'i hA/_spyan ma la sogs pa'i lha mo rnams kyi lAM mAM pAM tAM/_dzaHhUM baM hoH/_reg bya rdo rje ma'i khaM ngo /_/byams pa la sogs pa byang chub sems
[\[99b.7\]]dpa' brgyad po rnams kyi mai th+liM/_oM oM oM hUM oM saM ngo /_/khro bo bcu po rnams kyi hUM ngo /_/lha rnams kyi snying po'i sngags ni rdo rje phreng bar brjod do/_/rigs kyi bdag po ni mi bskyod pa dang kun du bzang po gnyis kyi gong du brjod pa'i rdo rje sems dpa' ste/_'on kyang rdo rje dang 'khor lo dang /_pad+ma dang
[\[100a\]]
[\[100a.1\]]dril bu dang /_nor bu dang ral gri 'dzin pa/_rang 'dra ba'i rdo rje dbyings kyi dbang phyug mas yang dag par 'khyud pa'o/_/de bzhin gshegs pa rnams dang mA ma kI dang /_phyag na rdo rje dang 'jam dpal dang gtsug tor 'khor los sgyur ba dang /_gnod mdzes rgyal po rnams kyi ni mi bskyod
[\[100a.2\]]pa'o/_/spyan ma dang gzugs rdo rje ma dang /_byams pa dang sa'i snying po dang gshin rje gshed dang mi g.yo ba rnams kyi rnam par snang mdzad do/_/sgra rdo rje ma dang nam mkha'i snying po dang /_shes rab mthar byed dang 'dod pa'i rgyal po rnams kyi ni rin chen 'byung ldan no/_/gos dkar mo dang /_dri rdo rje ma dang spyan
[\[100a.3\]]ras gzigs dang pad+ma mthar byed dang dbyug pa sngon po rnams kyi ni snang ba mtha' yas so/_/sgrol ma dang ro rdo rje ma dang reg bya rdo rje ma dang sgrib pa rnam par sel ba dang /_bgegs mthar byed dang /_stobs po che rnams kyi ni don yod grub pa'o/_/rgyas 'debs kyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad ni rang
[\[100a.4\]]'od kyi yum dang bcas pa'o/_/dpal kun tu kha sbyor gyi rgyud las gsungs pa'i rdo rje sems dpa'i dkyil 'khor ni rdo rje gur gyi nang du srung ba'i 'khor lo'i lte ba'i dbus su rlung dang me dang chu dang sa'i dkyil 'khor dang ri rab kyi steng du chos 'byung gi dkyil du gzhal yas khang ngo /_/srung ba'i 'khor
[\[100a.5\]]lor gshin rje gshed phyag g.yas pa gsum gyis rdo rje lcags kyu dang 'khor lo dang /_rdo rje rnams bsnams pa/_g.yon gsum gyis snying gar sdigs mdzub dang bcas pa'i zhags pa dang dril bu dang dgra sta 'dzin pa'o/_/shes rab mthar byed ni rdo rje zhags pa dang /_rdo rje dang ral gri dang snying
[\[100a.6\]]gar sdigs mdzub dang dril bu dang dgra sta 'dzin pa'o/_/pad+ma mthar byed ni lcags sgrog dang pad+ma dang ral gri dang /_dril bu dang dgra sta dang zhags pa'o/_/bgegs dgra ni rdo rje dril bu dang rdo rje rgya gram dang 'khor lo dang /_snying gar sdigs mdzub dang bcas pa'i zhags pa dang gtun shing dang
[\[100a.7\]]dgra sta'o/_/mi g.yo ba ni ral gri dang 'khor lo dang rdo rje dang sdigs mdzub dang dgra sta dang zhags pa'o/_/'dod pa'i rgyal po ni g.yas dang cig shos kyi phyag gnyis kyis rdo rje hUM mdzad kyi phyag rgya dang lcags kyu dang ral gri dang rdo rje dang zhags pa'o/_/dbyug pa sngon po ni rdo rjes mtshan pa'i
[\[100b\]]
[\[100b.1\]]dbyug pa sngon po dang /_ral gri dang 'khor lo dang sdigs mdzub dang bcas pa'i zhags pa dang pad+ma dang dgra sta'o/_/stobs po che ni rtse gsum pa dang ral gri dang 'khor lo dang /_snying gar sdigs mdzub dang bcas pa'i zhags pa dang pad+ma dang dgra sta'o/_/gtsug tor 'khor los sgyur ba
[\[100b.2\]]ni g.yas dang cig shos kyi phyag dang po gnyis kyis spyi bor gtsug tor gyi phyag rgya dang 'khor lo dang pad+ma dang sdigs mdzub dang ral gri'o/_/gnod mdzes ni rdo rje dang 'khor lo dang rin po che dang /_snying gar sdigs mdzub dang bcas pa'i zhags pa dang pad+ma dang ral gri'o/_/bcu po
[\[100b.3\]]'di dag ni dbu la thod pa lngas brgyan pa 'khor lo la sogs pa'i phyag rgya lnga dang ldan pa mi mgo'i phreng ba ske la 'chang ba go rims bzhin du rnam par snang mdzad dang rin chen 'byung ldan dang 'od dpag med dang don yod grub pa dang rtag pa dang rin chen 'byung ldan dang 'od dpag med dang don yod grub pa
[\[100b.4\]]pa dang mi bskyod pa dang mi bskyod pas rgyas btab pa'o/_/gzhal yas khang gi dbus su rdo rje sems dpa' zhal 'dzum pa dang bcas pa'i sku mdog dkar po la cung zad dmar ba'i mdangs dang ldan pa ral pa'i thor cog nag po la gnas pa'i nor bu dang sna tshogs rdo rje dang de'i 'og tu g.yon ngos su

[\[100b.7\]]pa 'dzin pa nyi ma'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor can sna tshogs pad+ma dang thod pa dang zla ba'i gdan la skyil krung phyed pas bzhugs pa gar gyi nyams dgu dang ldan pa'o/_/de'i thugs kar sna tshogs pad+ma dang zla ba la ye shes sems dpa' sku mdog dkar dmar sems dpa'i skyil krung can sangs rgyas lnga'i cod
[\[101a\]]
[\[101a.1\]]pan gyis spras pa rin po che'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa rdo rje dang rdo rje dril bu dang bcas pa'i phyag gnyis kyis/_rang dang 'dra ba'i shes rab la 'khyud pa/_de'i thugs kar zla ba la ting nge 'dzin sems dpa'i rang bzhin hUM nag po'i rnam pa'o/_/'dir sems dpa' gsum gyi bdag

[\[101a.5\]]ral gri dang rdo rje dang 'khor lo dang /_rin po che dang pad+ma'o/_/g.yon pa rnams kyis gzhu dang lcags kyu dang dril bu dang zhags pa dang thod pa dang kha T+wAM ga'o/_/bden bral du gos dkar mo dmar mo phyag brgyad ma g.yas rnams kyis mda' dang pad+ma dang ral gri dang rdo rje rnams so/_/g.yon pa rnams

[\[101b\]]
[\[101b.1\]]phyag na ral gri dang rdo rje dang chus gang ba'i thod pa dang dril bu'o/_/byang du rdo rje zhi ba ma ljang gu ni phyag na tal pa thung ngu dang ba dan gsum pa dang rdo rjes mtshan pa'i kha T+wAM ga dang sman gyis gang ba'i thod pa rnams so/_/dbang ldan du rdo rje gnod sbyin ma ni dkar ser gyi mdog la phyag na dbyug to dang ut+pal
[\[101b.2\]]dang thod pa dang Da ma ru'o/_/mer rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma dmar ser phyag na pad+ma dang me long dang rkang mar gyis gang ba'i thod pa dang dgra sta'o/_/bden bral du sgra rdo rje ma sngon dmar phyag na shak+ti dang dung dang 'khor lo dang khrag gis gang ba'i thod pa'o/_/rlung dus rdo rje ma dkar ljang pad+ma dang rdo rje dang bdud rtsi
[\[101b.3\]]lnga dang sha lngas gang ba'i thod pa mi lpags kyis g.yogs pa dang dril bu'o/_/brgyad po 'di dag ni phyag bzhi pa dang po'i phyag mtshan gnyis ni g.yas pa dag gis 'dzin pa gzhan gnyis ni g.yon pa dag gis 'dzin pa'o/_/rim pa gsum pa'i shar du bzhad ma dmar mo phyag gnyis rdo rje dang rdo rje
[\[101b.4\]]dril bu dang bcas pas mngon par bzhad pa'i tshul can no/_/lhor sgeg mo sngon po phyag gnyis rdo rje dang rdo rje dril bu 'dzin pas snyems pa dang bcas pas mngon par sgeg pa'i tshul can no/_/nub tu glu ma ser mo ni sku cung zad g.yo zhing sgeg pa'i phyag gnyis kyis ting ting shag 'dzin pa'o/_/
[\[101b.5\]]byang du gar ma ljang gu pad skor gyi tshul la sogs pa'i gar gyis g.yo ba'i phyag gnyis kyis rdo rje rtse gsum pa dang rdo rje dril bu 'dzin pa'o/_/dbang ldan du gling bu ma dmar mo'o/_/mer pi wang ma ser mo phyag gnyis ma sgeg mo'i nyams kyis bag tsam lus g.yo ba'o/_/bden bral du mu kun+da ma
[\[101b.6\]]dkar mo'o/_/rlung du rdza rnga ma du ba'i mdog can no/_/bzhi po 'di dag ni phyag gnyis kyis rang rang gi rol cha brdung ba'o/_/de nas phyi'i snam bu la me'i mtshams su me tog ma dkar mo phyag g.yon gyis me tog gi phreng ba dang cig shos kyis 'khor lo 'dzin pa'o/_/bden bral du bdug spos ma

[\[102a.1\]]gri 'dzin pa'o/_/shar gyi phyogs su me long ma dkar mo phyag gnyis kyis me long 'dzin pa'o/_/lhor ro ma dmar mo phyag gnyis kyis ro'i snod 'dzin pa'o/_/nub tu reg ma ljang gu phyag gnyis kyis gos sna tshogs 'dzin pa'o/_/byang du chos ma dkar mo phyag gnyis kyis

[\[103b.1\]]byed pa'o/_/bzhi po 'di dag ni sna tshogs pad+ma la gnas pa'i yi dwags kyi snying gar nyi ma'i gdan la bzhugs pa'o/_/rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma la sogs pa bcu gnyis ni zhal gcig la spyan gsum pa'o/_/lha mo bcu gsum po thams cad kyang lha'i gos dmar po mnabs pa dbu

[\[112a.1\]]phag mo gnyis kyis gser gyi mdog gam sngon pos yang ste/_bcom ldan 'das ni phyag g.yas pas rdo rje gsor ba la mchog tu brtson pa g.yon pas thod pa dang kha T+wAM ga 'dzin pa'am/_yang na rdo rje dang dril bu'i phyag gnyis kyis 'khyud pas gnas pa'o/_/DA ki ma la

[\[112a.3\]]pad+ma'i dril bu 'dzin pa'o/_/DA ki ma rnams ni nag mo phyag g.yas pa na pad+ma dang bcas pa'i sdigs mdzub mdzad pa'o/_/sku'i 'khor lo'i dpa' bo rnams ni dkar po 'khor lo dang 'khor lo'i dril bu 'dzin pa'o/_/lha mo rnams ni dmar mo g.yas pas sdigs mdzub dang bcas pa'i 'khor
[\[112a.4\]]lo 'dzin pa rnams so/_/dpa' bo thams cad ni yum la 'khyud par brtson pa g.yas brkyang gis bzhugs pa rnams so/_/dpa' mo rnams ni de'i brla gnyis la 'khril ba'i tshul lo/_/khwa gdong ma la sogs pa rnams ni g.yas sdigs mdzub dang bcas pa'i gri gug 'dzin pa'o/_/lha mo thams
[\[112a.5\]]cad ni g.yon pas thod pa 'dzin pa'o/_/gshin rje brtan ma la sogs pa ni g.yas pas DA ma ru g.yon pas sdigs mdzub dang bcas pa'i mi mgo 'dzin pa'o/_/DA ki ma la sogs pa rnams dang khwa gdong ma la sogs pa rnams kyi g.yon pa'i dpung pa la kha T+wAM ga'o/_/bcu gnyis po 'di
[\[112a.6\]]rnams ni skyil krung phyed pa'i gar gyis gnas pa khyad par gzhan thams cad ni gong bzhin no/_/'di ni bde mchog gi dkyil 'khor rnam pa gsum mo//_//gang gi tshe 'di rnams la dpa' bo nyi shu rtsa lnga mi bsgom par rdo rje phag mo dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bor gyur pa de'i tshe rdo rje phag mo'i dkyil 'khor
[\[112a.7\]]gsum mo/_/rdo rje phag mo'i snying ga'i sa bon ni baM mo/_/oM badzra bai ro tsa nI ye hUM hUM hUM phaT ces pa ni snying po'o/_/bde mchog gi phyag gnyis pa la sogs pa lha 'di rnams kyi phyag g.yas su gnas pa'i phyag mtshan ni bri bya'i dkyil 'khor la bri bar bya'o//_//bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas thod
[\[112b\]]
[\[112b.1\]]pa lha nyi shu rtsa lnga'i bdag nyid can gyi dkyil 'khor la rdo rje gur gyi nang du chos 'byung gi dbus su gnas pa'i gzhal yas khang gi nang du 'khor lo rtsibs brgyad pa nag po la gnas pa'i sna tshogs pad+ma 'dab brgyad kyi ze 'brur ro/_/gan rkyal gyi snying gar nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor la bcom ldan
[\[112b.2\]]'das dpal he ru ka sku mdog nag po skyil krung phyed pa gar gyi nyams dgus gar byed pa zhal gcig pa phyag bzhi pa spyan gsum dmar la zlum pa g.yas kyi phyag gnyis na DA ma ru dang gri gug g.yon gyi phyag gnyis na thod pa dang kha T+wAM ga 'dzin pa'o/_/phyag rgya drug pa mi mgo rlon pa lnga bcu'i

[\[113a\]]
[\[113a.1\]]la ni 'khor lo dkar po rtsibs brgyad pa la gnas pa'i pad+ma brgyad de rdo rje dkar po'i phreng bas bskor ba'o/_/de'i shar gyi rtsibs la sgrol ma'o/_/byang du 'jigs mthong ma'o/_/nub tu legs mthong ma'o/_/lhor thub dka' ma'o/_/dbang ldan du dge

[\[113b\]]
[\[113b.1\]]gnas pa'i gzhal yas khang gi dkyil du dbus kyi rim pa'i lte bar seng ge'i steng du sna tshogs pad+ma dang zla ba la sems dpa'i skyil krung gis bzhugs pa'i bcom ldan 'das dpal rnal 'byor nam mkha' nag po rtsa ba dang g.yas g.yon gyi zhal gsum nag po dang dkar po dang dmar po

[\[114a\]]
[\[114a.1\]]pa 'dzin pa'i phyag gnyis so/_/rlung du ce spyang gi gdan la tsog pur bzhugs pa'i 'ug pa ma 'ug pa'i gdong can dmar ser mo phyag gnyis kyis dbyug pa dang zhags pa 'dzin pa'o/_/'di rnams ni rang rang gi chibs rnams la pad+ma dang nyi mar gnas pa'o/_/shar du rdo rje

[\[120a\]]
[\[120a.1\]]pa phang pa'i steng du bzhag pa ting nge 'dzin gyi phyag rgya'i g.yas pa'i gung mos rdo rjes mtshan pa'i pad+ma 'dzin pa'o/_/shar gyi 'dab mar rdo rje chos dmar skya g.yon pa 'gying ba'i tshul dang bcas pas pad+ma'i yu ba 'dzin cing g.yas pas kha 'byed pa'o/_/lho ru rdo rje rnon

[\[120a.3\]]chos kyi 'khor lo'i phyag rgya 'dzin pa'o/_/nub tu rdo rje smra ba dmar po g.yon pa chos kyi dung dang g.yas pas rdo rje rtse gcig pa'i lce 'dzin pa'o/_/byang du khyung gi steng du sna tshogs pad+ma'i lte bar don yod grub pa ljang gu rdo rje skyil krung gis bzhugs pa/_phyag g.yas pa'i gung mos sna tshogs
[\[120a.4\]]rdo rje 'dzin pas mi 'jigs pa sbyin pa'i tshul byed cing g.yon pa gan rkyal du pang bar bzhag pa'o/_/shar gyi 'dab mar rdo rje las ljang gu g.yas pas snying gar bslang ba'i sbyor bas sna tshogs rdo rje rtse mo bcu gnyis pa 'dzin pa/_g.yon pa sna tshogs rdo rjes mtshan pa'i dril bu dkur
[\[120a.5\]]brten pa/_yang na lag pa gnyis kyis thal mo spyi bor sbyar nas sna tshogs rdo rje spyi bor 'dzin pa'o/_/lhor rdo rje bsrung ba ser po phyag gnyis kyi rdo rje'i go cha 'dzin pa'o/_/byang du rdo rje gnod sbyin nag po phyag gnyis kyis mthe chung gnyis kyi rdo rje mche ba'i mtshon gyi rtse mo gnyis rang gi khar
[\[120a.6\]]bcug pas gdug pa rnams sdigs par byed pa'o/_/nub tu rdo rje khu tshur ser po khu tshur gyi mtshams su rdo rje ste/_rdo rje khu tshur dag gis bzung ba'i rdo rje rtse lnga pa bsdams pa'o/_/dbus kyi gzhal yas khang gi me'i pad+ma rdo rje sgeg mo dkar mo rdo rje dkur brten pa'i phyag rgya'i
[\[120a.7\]]phyag gnyis kyis rdo rje gnyis 'dzin pa'o/_/bden bral du pad+ma la phreng ba ma ser mo phyag gnyis kyis rat+na'i phreng ba 'dzin pa'o/_/rlung du pad+ma la glu ma dmar mo phyag gnyis kyis pi wang gi rgyud sbreng ba'o/_/dbang ldan du pad+ma la gar ma ljang gu rdo rje rtse gsum pa gnyis bzung
[\[120b\]]
[\[120b.1\]]nas phyag gnyis kyis gar byed pa'o/_/dbus kyi gzhal yas khang gi phyi ru snam bu la shar du pad+ma rnams la byams pa dang mthong ba don yod dang ngan song kun 'dren dang /_mya ngan dang mun pa thams cad 'joms pa'i blo gros rnams ni mi bskyod ba lta bu'o/_/lhor pad+ma rnams la spos kyi
[\[120b.2\]]glang po dang /_dpa' bar 'gro ba dang /_nam mkha' mdzod dang /_ye shes tog rnams ni rin chen 'byung ldan lta bu'o/_/nub tu pad+ma rnams la 'od dpag med dang /_zla ba'i 'od dang bzang skyong dang dra ba can gyi 'od rnams ni 'od dpag med lta bu'o/_/byang du pad+ma rnams la rdo rje snying po dang /_blo
[\[120b.3\]]gros mi bzad pa dang /_spobs pa brtsegs pa dang /_kun du bzang po rnams ni don yod grub pa lta bu'o/_/yang na shar la sogs pa'i snam bu rnams la bskal pa bzang po'i byang chub sems dpa' byams pa la sogs pa stong du bzhis mtshang ba bsgom par bya'o/_/de'i mtshan rnams
[\[120b.4\]]mangs pas 'jigs pas ma bshad do/_/me'i mtshams su pad+ma la rdo rje bdug sbos ma dkar mo dang bden bral gyi pad+ma la rdo rje me tog ma ser po dang /_rlung gi pad+ma la rdo rje mar me ma dkar dmar dang /_dbang ldan gyi pad+ma la rdo rje dri chab ma ljang gu/_bdug spos ma la sogs pa 'di
[\[120b.5\]]rnams gang bzhin du phyag mtshan 'dzin pa'o/_/shar la sogs pa'i sgo'i pad+ma rnams la rdo rje lcags kyu dang rdo rje zhags pa dang /_rdo rje lcags sgrog dang /_rdo rje 'bebs pa rnams rim pa bzhin du dkar po dang ser po dang dmar po dang ljang gu rnams ni gong bzhin du phyag mtshan 'dzin pa'o/_/

[\[120b.7\]]sems dpa' bcu drug ni rang gi rigs kyi bdag po de bzhin gshegs pa la mngon du phyogs pa'o/_/rnam par snang mdzad la sogs pa nas rdo rje 'bebs pa'i bar gyi lha rnams ni ji ltar gsungs pa'i lte ba dang 'dab ma rnams la gnas shing nyi ma'i 'od zer can no/_/de bzhin gshegs
[\[121a\]]
[\[121a.1\]]pa lnga las gzhan pa'i lha bzhi bcu zhe brgyad ni sems dpa'i skyil krung gis bzhugs pa'o/_/'dir bcom ldan 'das rdo rje dbyings rnam par snang mdzad shin tu rnam par dag pa'i chos kyi dbyings kyi ye shes kyi bdag nyid la rang 'dra ba'i rdo rje sems dpas rgyas btab pa'o/_/

[\[121a.4\]]dang /_'od dpag med la sogs pa bzhi dang /_rdo rje lcags sgrog rnams kyi snang ba mtha' yas so/_/las kyi rdo rje ma dang /_rdo rje las la sogs pa bzhi dang /_gar ma dang dri chab ma dang /_rdo rje snying po la sogs pa bzhi dang rdo rje 'bebs pa rnams kyi don yod grub pa'o/_/'dir nang
[\[121a.5\]]gi gzhal yas khang gi sgo rnams su'ang /_rdo rje lcags kyu la sogs pa sgo skyong bzhi bsgom par bya'o zhes pa phyogs gzhan no/_/rnam par snang mdzad kyi snying ga'i sa bon AHoM sarba ta thA ga tA ma hA yo gI shwa ra hUM zhes pa ni snying po'o/_/oM badzra yak+Sha hUM zhes pa ni rdo rje gnod sbyin gyi las

[\[121b\]]
[\[121b.1\]]yas khang zhes pa ni phyogs gnyis pa'o/_/phyogs gnyis ka la yang mchod rten dkar po'i nang du gzhal yas khang ngo /_/de'i lte ba la seng ge'i steng du sna tshogs pad+ma dang zla ba la sems dpa'i skyil krung gis bzhugs pa'i bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi rang bzhin 'jam pa'i rdo rje

[\[121b.3\]]rnams kyis shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i pu sti dang chu skyes sngon po dang gzhu 'dzin pa'o/_/bdag lta bu'i rdo rje dbyings kyi dbang phyug ma la snyoms par zhugs pa'o/_/de'i shar phyogs kyi le tshe la glang po che'i steng du sna tshogs pad+ma dang nyi ma la mi bskyod pa sngon po 'gying ba'i tshul gyis gnas pa

[\[121b.5\]]kyis nu ma dang zhags pa dang gzhu 'dzin pa'o/_/lho ru rta'i steng du sna tshogs chu skyes dang nyi ma la rin chen 'byung ldan ser po sems dpa'i skyil krung gis bzhugs pa/_ser po dang sngon po dang dkar po rtsa ba dang g.yas g.yon gyi zhal lo/_/phyag drug pa rtsa ba'i phyag dag gis mnyam gzhag gi

[\[122a\]]
[\[122a.1\]]gi steng du sna tshogs chu skyes dang nyi ma la don yod grub pa sems dpa'i skyil krung gis bzhugs pa kha dog dmar po dmar po dang sngon po dang dkar po rtsa ba dang g.yas g.yon gyi zhal lo/_/phyag drug pa dang po gnyis kyis bsam gtan gyi phyag rgya bcing ba'o/_/g.yas pa gnyis

[\[122b.1\]]lcags kyu dang rdo rje dang ba dan gsum gyi tshul dang bgrang phreng ngo /_/g.yon pa rnams kyis yid bzhin gyi nor bu'i rgyal mtshan dang /_pad+ma dang spyi blugs dang zhags pa dang gzhu dang shag ti dang 'khor lo dang ral gri dang sdigs mdzub dang bum pa bzang po dang bi di ba la dang /_shes rab kyi pha

[\[123a.1\]]sna 'dzin pa'o/_/g.yas kyi mchog sbyin no/_/ye shes tog ser po g.yon pas yid bzhin gyi nor bu'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa'o/_/g.yas mchog sbyin no/_/lho ru bzang skyong sku mdog dmar po/_/g.yon pa rat+na 'dzin pa g.yas pas mchog sbyin no/_/blo gros

[\[123a.7\]]dang zla ba'i 'od can no/_/sems dpa'i skyil krung gis bzhugs pa spyan gsum pa rang phyogs kyi bdag po bzhin du zhal gsum pa phyag drug pa phyag gnyis kyis mnyam gzhag gi phyag rgya byas pa/_gnyis kyis gzhu dang mda' 'dzin pa'o/_/byams pa dang 'jam dbyangs gnyis

[\[123b.1\]]la ni mnyam gzhag gi phyag rgya med do/_/'jam pa'i rdo rje la sogs pa'i lha thams cad gos sna tshogs pa dang rin po che'i rgyan dang ral ba'i thor tshugs dang 'dzum pa dang bcas pa'i zhal dang sgeg pa'i nyams dang ldan pa'o/_/shar gyi sgor ma he'i steng du gshin rje mthar byed nag po phyag

[\[124a.1\]]ral gri dang dgra ste dang mda' 'dzin pa'o/_/g.yon pa rnams kyis sdigs mdzub dang bcas pa'i zhags pa dang nu ma dang gzhu 'dzin pa'o/_/dbang ldan gyi mtshams su rat+na'i ri bo'i steng du mi g.yo ba sngon po phyag drug pa g.yas pa rnams kyis ral gri dang zhags
[\[124a.2\]]pa dang mda' 'dzin pa'o/_/g.yon pa rnams kyis sdigs mdzub dang bcas pa'i zhags pa dang nu ma dang gzhu 'dzin pa'o/_/g.yon ngos su 'phyang ba'i gos sngon po 'dzin pa'o/_/khrag gis brlan pa'i ljags 'gul ba'i zhal gdangs pa'o/_/mer 'dod pa'i rgyal po sngon po phyag

[\[124a.5\]]g.yas pa rnams kyis rdo rje dang dbyug pa dang ral gri dang mda'o/_/g.yon pa rnams kyis sdigs mdzub dang bcas pa'i zhags pa dang nu ma dang tho ba dang gzhu 'dzin pa'o/_/dkyil 'khor gyi dbang phyug gi steng du gnod mdzes rgyal po sngon po phyag gnyis kyis rdo rje hUM mdzad kyi
[\[124a.6\]]phyag rgya bcings pa g.yas pa gnyis kyis ral gri dang mda' 'dzin pa'o/_/g.yon pa gnyis kyis nu ma dang gzhu 'dzin pa'o/_/'dir 'dod pa'i rgyal po'i phyag rgya de nyid kyi mdzub mo gnyis gyen du bsgreng ba ni gnod mdzes kyi phyag rgya'o/_/'og tu rdo rje sa 'og sngon po phyag drug pa
[\[124a.7\]]g.yas pa rnams kyis rdo rje dang lcags kyu dang mda' 'dzin pa'o/_/g.yon pa rnams kyis nu ma dang zhags pa dang bcas pa'i rtse gcig pa dang gzhu 'dzin pa'o/_/bgegs mthar byed la sogs pa bdun po ni sngon po dang ser po dang dmar po rtsa ba dang g.yas g.yon gyi zhal gsum
[\[124b\]]
[\[124b.1\]]mo/_/khro bo bcu yang khros pa'i lta stangs can spyan dmar po smin ma g.yo ba bag tsam rtsa ba'i zhal kha phye ba/_g.yas pa'i zhal gdangs ba/_g.yon pa'i zhal ma mchu mnan pa mche ba gtsigs pa stag gi pags pas smad dang stod la gon pa thod pa'i phreng bas dbu la brgyan
[\[124b.2\]]pa/_dbu skra 'bar ba gyen la bcings shing 'khyil ba sma ra dmar ser rol pa'i kun tu bskyod pa can/_klu'i rgyal po brgyad kyis brgyan pa/_phud kyi sgra sgrogs pa dang bcas pa'i gdengs ka can rnams kyis 'jigs pa sna tshogs pad+ma dang /_nyi ma'i gdan la g.yon brkyang

[\[125a.1\]]bu'i shes rab ma la snyoms par zhugs pa rnams kyi'o/_/khro bo rnams kyis ni bdag lta bu'i shes rab ma g.yon ngos su gnas pa'i nu ma 'dzin pa'o zhes shes par bya'o/_/gshin rje mthar byed las gzhan rnams la shes rab ma med kyang de'i nu mar 'dzin

[\[128a.1\]]dang sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel ba ljang gu ste rdo rje rtse gsum pas mtshan pa'i pad+ma dkar dmar 'dzin pa'o/_/ye shes mi zad pa'i zla ma tog dmar mo rat+na'i za me tog 'dzin pa'o/_/sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos kyi mdzod mo ser mo pad+ma la gnas

[\[128a.6\]]pa dang sgeg pa'i nyams dang ldan pa sna tshogs pad+ma dang zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la sems dpa'i skyil krung gis bzhugs pa'o/_/khyad par du sgo skyong ma rnams ni nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor la bzhugs pa'o/_/gzhan ni de rnams kyang zla ba la gnas pa'o zhes so/_/dkyil 'khor gsum pa

[\[128b.1\]]'jigs pas pad+ma 'dzin pa'o/_/sa'i snying po ser po g.yas pas sa gnon mdzad pa/_g.yon pas pad+ma la gnas pa'i dpag bsam gyi shing 'dzin pa'o/_/nam mkha'i snying po ljang gu g.yas pas rat+na sna tshogs kyi char 'bebs pa/_g.yon pas yid bzhin gyi nor bu 'dzin

[\[133a.3\]]nub dmar po byang ljang gu'o zhes gsungs so/_/'khor lo'i lte ba la sna tshogs pad+ma la gnas pa'i seng ge'i steng du bcom ldan 'das shAkya seng ge rnam par snang mdzad chen po shin tu gser gyi mdog can chos kyi 'khor lo'i phyag rgya mdzad pa'o/_/shar gyi rtsibs la rdo rje gtsug
[\[133a.4\]]tor dkar pos gnon gyi phyag rgya can no/_/lho'i rtsibs la rin chen gtsug tor sngon po mchog sbyin gyi phyag rgya mdzad pa'o/_/nub kyi rtsibs la pad+ma gtsug tor dmar po bsam gtan gyi phyag rgya can no/_/byang gi rtsibs la sna tshogs gtsug tor ljang gu mi 'jigs pa rab tu sbyin pa'i
[\[133a.5\]]phyag rgya'o/_/me'i rtsibs la gtsug tor gzi brjid sku mdog dkar dmar phyag gnyis kyis nyi ma 'dzin pa phyag g.yon pa dkur brten pa'o/_/bden bral gyi rtsibs la gtsug tor rgyal mtshan sku mdog dmar nag 'dres pas phyag gnyis kyis yid bzhin gyi nor bu'i rgyal mtshan

[\[223b.6\]]lte ba'i dkyil 'khor du bsgom bya/_/aM yig ye shes las legs byang /_/mchog tu mtha' yas dga' byed ma'o/_/dam tshig sems dpa' rdzogs byas la/_/ye shes sems dpa' bsgom par bya/_/zla drug sbyor ba goms pa yis/_/shes rab pha rol phyin mar 'gyur/_/zhag bdun na ni rab sbyor bas/_/bstan bcos kun
[\[223b.7\]]la 'jigs med 'gyur/_/'bum phrag bzlas pa'i sbyor ba yis/_/nyin re tshigs bcad brgyad brgya byed/_/rab tu brtson pa dag gis kyang /_/gzhung ni brgya yang 'dzin par byed/_/'di la sngags kyi tshig tu gyur pa rnams ni/_oM pi tsu pi cu pra dz+nyA bar+d+ha ni dz+wa la dz+wa la me d+ha bar+d+ha ni d+hi ri d+hi ri bud+hi bar+d+ha ni swA hA sngags 'dis ma stsal ba'i sbrang rtsi la
[\[224a\]]
[\[224a.1\]]lan bdun mngon par bsngags nas ji srid zla ba drug gi bar du sbu gus 'thungs pas shes rab chen por 'gyur ro/_/oM pi swA hA sngags 'di la yang mi bskyod pas rgyas gdab par bya ba yin no/_/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgrub thabs so/_/paN+Di ta chen po ma la ba zhes bya ba d+ha byang chub sems dpa'i zhal snga nas dge
[\[224a.2\]]slong tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//[ {D3222}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_pradz+nyA pA ra mi tA sA d+ha naM/_bod skad du/_shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma'i sgrub thabs/_sngar bshad pa'i cho gas rang gi snying gar pad+ma dkar po 'dab ma dang ldan pa'i zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la yi ge praM dkar po rnam par bkod de/_/de nyid las sngar
[\[224a.3\]]bzhin du thams cad tshul bzhin du byas nas yi ge praM dang pad+ma yongs su gyur pa las bcom ldan 'das ma zhal gcig phyag gnyis ma sku mdog dkar mo ste/_lung dang rtogs pa'i bdag nyid kyis rin po che'i dbu rgyan gyis brgyan pa/_shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i po tis mtshan pa'i pad+ma can gnyis g.yas pa dang g.yon
[\[224a.4\]]pa'i zur gyi bar snang la langs la legs par bsnams pa phyag gnyis kyis chos bshad pa'i phyag rgya bcings shing /_pad+ma dkar po dang zla ba la rdo rje skyil mo krung gis bzhugs pa/_gzhon shing lang tsho la bab pa dregs pa dang ldan pa/_na bza' dang rgyan rnam par bkra ba rnams kyis brgyan pa/_so sor snang ba tsam du rab tu spro
[\[224a.5\]]bar byed pa'i 'od zer gyi tshogs rnam pa sna tshogs kyis nam mkha' kun nas 'gengs par byed pa mar me'i phreng ba dang 'dra ba thogs pa med pa'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma du ma spro ba dang bsdu ba'i sbyor bas thams cad rang bzhin gcig tu lhag par mos pas kyang ji srid du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma mngon sum
[\[224a.6\]]du byas pa de srid du bsgom par bya ba'o/_/de nas yang gang gi tshe rgod par gyur na de'i tshe sna'i rtse mo la pad+ma dkar po sran ma tsa na ka'i tshad tsam bris pa dang 'dra ba rnam par bsgoms la/_de la gnas pa'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma shin tu phra mor gyur pa sngar bshad pa'i gzugs rtse gcig gis yid kyi dus
[\[224a.7\]]yongs su chad pa med par yang dang yang du bsgom par bya ba'o/_/de nas bskyed pa'i phyogs kyi sngags ni oM praM swA hA/_rdzogs pa'i phyogs kyi sngags ni yod pa yin te/_don dam pa'i rim pa'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma'i rnal 'byor gyi gdams ngag thob par gyur pa/_dge 'dun gyi bu zhes pa/_rigs ming yang
[\[224b\]]
[\[224b.1\]]ste brtson pa yis/_/sgrub thabs gsal por bris pa ni/_/sems can thams cad don phyir yin/_/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgrub thabs so/_/a b+ha ya'i zhal snga nas dge slong tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//[ {D3223}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_sar swa ti swA d+ha naM/_bod skad du/_dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs/_dbyangs
[\[224b.2\]]can ma la phyag 'tshal lo/_/sngon du brjod pa'i rim pa dag gis ji srid du stong pa nyid mngon du byas shing byin gyis kyang brlabs la/_pad+ma dkar po khru bdun gyi tshad do/_/de'i steng du zla ba'i dkyil 'khor ro/_/de'i dbus su yi ge hrIHdkar po ste/_des pad+ma dkar po rang gi sa bon gyi snying po can du bsgom par bya'o/_/de las kyang
[\[224b.3\]]bcom ldan 'das ma dbyangs can ma chen mo rjes su bsam par bya ba'o/_/ston ka'i zla ba'i rnam pa ltar snang ba pad+ma dkar po'i steng na zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la bzhugs pa/_phyag g.yas pa mchog sbyin par mdzad cing /_g.yon pas pad+ma dkar po yu ba dang ldan pa bsnams pa/_bzhin 'dzum pa dang ldan zhing /_mchog tu
[\[224b.4\]]thugs rje'i rang bzhin can/_/tsan+dan dang me tog dang na bza' dkar po dang ldan pa/_mu tig gi do shal gyis thugs ka nas mdzes par gyur pa/_rin po che sna tshogs kyi rgyan dang ldan pa/_lo bcu gnyis mi'i tshad du gyur pa/_rked pa'i skabs dga' bar gyur pa/_yangs la mdzes pa'i brang lcong zhing phyal ba/_'od zer gyi bkod pa
[\[224b.5\]]mtha' yas pa spro bar mdzad pas 'jig rten gsum kun du snang bar mdzad pa/_de nas de'i mdun du ni bcom ldan 'das shes rab ma'o/_/g.yas su ni yid gzhungs ma'o/_/rgyab tu ni blo gros ma'o/_/g.yon du ni dran pa ma'o/_/de dag rnams ni rang gi gtso mo dang kha dog la sogs pa mtshungs pa dang /_mngon du blta bas
[\[224b.6\]]gnas par bsam par bya ba'o/_/de nas rang gi lte ba'i yul phyogs su zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la yi ge oM dkar po bsgom par bya ba'o/_/de las lhag ma ma lus pa'i ngag gi rang bzhin gyi phreng ba nges par 'phros par gyur pas rgyun mi 'chad par rab tu 'byung bar bsam par bya zhing sngags bgrang bar bya ba'o/_/de la
[\[224b.7\]]sngags ni 'di yin te/_oM hrIHma hA ma yAM ge ma hA sa ra swa t+ye na maHde ltar yang bsnyen gnas la gnas par gyur pa dang /_ngag mi smra bar gnas pa dang /_rtag par rgyun mi 'chad par lha'i nga rgyal gyis lhag par gnas pa dang /_sngags rgyun du zlos pa dang /_las gzhan la mi sems pas ni dbyangs can
[\[225a\]]
[\[225a.1\]]ma'i gsung 'thob pa'o/_/zla ba gsum na tshangs pa yang 'grub par 'gyur ro/_/zla ba drug na dbyangs can ma dang mnyam par 'gyur ba yin no/_/de nas sman bshad par bya ste/_ra 'o 'jigs med tsha gsum pa tha dang /_/shu dag si gu rgyam tsha rnams bsnyams la/_lan bdun mngon par bsngags te
[\[225a.2\]]mar sar dang /_/'thungs pas dbyangs can ma nyid 'grub pa yin/_/ra'o bzhi 'gyur dag tu bya ba yin/_/mar ni bskol ba srang gcig dag yin te/_/sman rnams srang re tsam du byas pas ni/_/dal gyis 'jam por ming ni blo gros bzang /_/zla ba tsam du rab tu sbyar byas pas/_/ngag gi dbang ni bla na med pa 'thob/_/zla ba drug tu
[\[225a.3\]]nye bar sbyar byas pas/_/dngos su ngag gi dbang phyug nyid du 'gyur/_/mnyam med khu byug skad ni nges sgrogs pa'i/_/snyan pa'i dbyangs ni skye bar 'gyur ba yin/_/dngos rnams sna tshogs pa yi nus ldan phyir/_/'di la the tshom za bar bya ba min/_/zhes bya ba ni dbyangs can ma chen mo'i sgrub thabs so/_/mkhas pa
[\[225a.4\]]a b+ha ya las dge slong tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//[ {D3224}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_badzra sA ra swa ti sA d+ha naM/_bod skad du/_rdo rje dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs/_sngar bshad pa'i cho ga'i tshul gyis snying gar pad+ma dmar po dang /_zla ba la yi ge ngoHdmar po'i sa bon yongs su gyur pa las
[\[225a.5\]]pad+ma dmar po 'dab ma brgyad pa rang gi sa bon gyi snying por gyur pa'o/_/de yongs su gyur pa las bcom ldan 'das dbyangs can ma ste/_zhal gsum phyag drug ma/_sku mdog thams cad dmar ba/_spyan gsum ma sngon po dang dkar po ni g.yas pa dang g.yon pa'i zhal lo/_/pad+ma dang ral gri dang gri gug g.yas pa'i phyag
[\[225a.6\]]na bsnams pa'o/_/thod pa dang rin po che dang 'khor lo ni g.yon pa'i phyag na bsnams pa'o/_/g.yas bskum pas gnas pa/_gzhon nu ma gsar zhing lang tsho dang ldan pa rgyan sna tshogs pa dang ldan pa/_mtshan ma dang sa bon gyis thugs ka nas byin gyis brlabs pa/_gzhan gyi don mdzad pa la brtson par gyur par bdag nyid
[\[225a.7\]]rnam par bsgom par bya ba'o/_/oM bi tsu pi tsu pradz+nyA bar+d+ha ni dz+wa la dz+wa la me d+ha bar+d+ha ni d+hi ri d+hi ri bu d+hi bar+d+ha ni swA hA/_zhes bya ba'i sngags 'di bzlas par bya ba'o/_/rdo rje dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs so/_/ma la ba zhes bya ba d+ha'i zhal snga nas dge slong tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//[ {D3225}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_

[\[225b.1\]]sa ra swa twi swa d+ha naM/_bod skad du/_dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs/_rdzogs sangs rgyas rnams gsung mnga'i 'od zer spro mdzad ngag ni mtshar ba'i ro dbyangs dang ldan pas/_/myang ba rnams la phan mdzad rgal dka' mi zad gti mug mun pa nye bar 'joms mdzad ma/_/yon tan rang bzhin rdo rje dbyangs can ma khyod la 'dud 'dir de'i
[\[225b.2\]]yan lag mnyes byed pa/_/blo gros rtogs dka'i dbang du byas nas 'gro la phan phyir bde bar gshegs lugs bshad par bya/_/dang po nyid du gdong sogs dag par byas la rab tu snga bar brtse ldan bzod pa can/_/byams pa mgu bas rangs pa'i dga' ba dang ldan gang yin sngags pas gtsang ma'i gos dang ni/_/
[\[225b.3\]]gnas kyang yid 'phrog par ni nyin yang rung ste rang gi snying gar pad+ma blta bar bya/_/der ni dri med a las nges par byung ba'i zla ba legs par bsgom bya de la yang /_/doHyig 'od zer gyis ni dgang bar bya dang phyogs mtha' kun du khyab bya de las ni/_/mdun du sangs rgyas tshogs rnams blta bya me tog la
[\[225b.4\]]sogs mchod la 'di dag bsgom par bya/_/de nas phyag 'tshal yang ni 'di yis sdig pa so sor bshags bya de bzhin bsod nams la/_/rjes su yi rang gsum la skyabs 'gro yang dag par ni brjod par bya ba'o sngags rig pas/_/zhes sogs bsngo byas par ni legs byas yang dag bdag nyid kyang
[\[225b.5\]]ste rtog pa'i dra ba ni/_/thams cad de yis stong par dmigs bya de nas sna tshogs 'di dag ma lus bsgom bya ba/_/gcig dang du bral dang ldan tshig ni brjod bya dag pa dam pa'i ye shes kyis rig bya/_/oM stong pa nyid kyi ye shes kyi rdo rje'i rang bzhin gyi bdag nyid ni nga yin no/_/stong nyid las
[\[225b.6\]]ni nges byung pad+ma zla ba dag la nyer gnas doHyig dmar po'o/_/yang ni sna tshogs 'od zer tshogs kyis shin tu mdzes gyur de las pad+ma 'dab brgyad pa/_/de las dmar mo 'od zer cher 'bar bcom ldan 'das ma dam pa'i rgyan rnams kyis brgyan ma/_/g.yas bskum pa yi zhabs kyis
[\[225b.7\]]gnas shing zhal gsum ma ste phyag drug dag gis brgyan pa mo/_/zhal g.yas mthing nag dang ni pad+ma ral gri gri gug rnams ni bsnams pas phyag rgyas shing /_/g.yon zhal dkar po dang ni de bzhin thod bcas rin chen dam pa dang ni 'khor lo bsnams/_/snying gi pad+ma la gnas zla ba'i dbus su

[\[226a.1\]]nyer gnas der yang doHni 'bar gyur pas/_/sna tshogs pa yi gti mug nye bar bcom par byas shing spros pa yis ni 'jig rten dag byas te/_/nye bar bsdus la rang snying zla ba sa bon la ni bzhag par blta bya yang ni spro/_/de nyid 'dir ni yud tsam yud tsam nyi ma re rer bsgom bya rtag tu
[\[226a.2\]]de lta ba'i/_/bsgoms byas skyon 'di yis 'dir ni sa bon tshogs pa legs par btang la 'di yi sngags/_/phreng ba brgyud pa mar me'i rnam pa'i rim pas snying por gyur pa'i sngags 'di 'dra ba bzlas/_/oM pi tsu pi tsu pradz+nyA bar+d+ha ni dz+wa la dz+wa la me d+ha bar+d+ha ni d+hi ri d+hi ri bud+hi bar+d+ha ni swA hA/_lha mo'i sku ni yid la
[\[226a.3\]]brtag bya rab tu dga' bas thun tshod rnams ni thams cad la/_/sngags ni legs bzla bde gshegs lugs kyis sems can don phyir 'di dag yongs su bsngo ba dang /_/dgos pa sgrub pa'i dbang gis bsam gtan la ni rtse gcig gnas par bya ba'o ji srid du/_/'bum phrag dag na ma rdzogs
[\[226a.4\]]pas te rdzogs par gyur pa dang ni las kyi rim pa yin/_/mi mthun phyogs kyi rnam pa thams cad nye bar bcom pa'i bsam gtan byas pa nyid na de/_/dkar po'i tshes gcig nas ni ji srid zla tshes gnas par gyur par rang gi yid dang ni/_/de srid nub re bzhin du legs par sbyar ba nyid bya ji srid
[\[226a.5\]]zla ba nya yi bar/_/mtshan mo de nyid la yang 'di ni grub thob rgyal bar dka' dang snyan dngags pa nyid 'gyur/_/bcom ldan 'das ma dpal ldan rdo rje dbyangs can ma de yang dag mnyes byed gang yin pa/_/dpal ldan nag po'i rgyal pos dpal ldan gshin rje gshed kyi rgyud nas nye bar bton
[\[226a.6\]]byas nas/_/sems can rnams ni don phyir mdzes bkod las byung bsod nams bdag gis thog mar thog gyur pa/_/des ni 'gro rnams nag po dang ni cha 'dra bzlog par dka' ba'i grub thob snyan dngags shog_/dpal 'dzin gyis byas sgrub thabs 'di/_/gal te sangs rgyas rnal 'byor pa/_/dpal
